### æ¡ˆä¾‹ 112ï¼šAnthropomorphic Superhero Character 

[åŸæ–‡é“¾æ¥](https://x.com/Kerroudjm/status/1937253913305948321)

<img src="cases/112/superhero_carrot.png" width="300" alt=""><br>
<sub>Image Â© 2025 <a href="https://github.com/highscore-ai">@highscore-ai</a>, <a href="https://creativecommons.org/licenses/by/4.0/">CC BY 4.0</a> â€¢ Prompt by <a href="https://x.com/Kerroudjm">@Kerroudjm</a></sub>

The lighting should be dramatic and studio-style, with a gradient background that complements the object's natural tones. The result should be fun, bold, detailed, and in 1:1 format.
```

    "reflections": true,
    "shadows": false,
    "transparency": true
  }
}
```
